# PATH MAP

<!--PATH_MAP kb=3DS filename_limit=80 repository_path_limit=197 -->

All knowledge content is preserved. Physical paths were shortened for reliable Windows download and extraction. Original vendor identifiers inside records remain unchanged.

- previous KB folder: `3DS_FULL_SYSTEM_DIGEST/`
- current KB folder: `3DS_KB/`
- shortened names use a readable prefix plus a deterministic SHA-256 suffix

## DIRECTORY ALIASES

| original relative directory | current relative directory |
|---|---|
| `SYSTEMS_MODELING_OFFICIAL_REPOSITORIES` | `SM_REPOS` |
